       ANDROID SMART E-PAYMENT SOLUTIONS

       安卓智能電子支付解決方案
       General features: Powered by Android operating system and PCI PTS certified. Compact, portable, equipped with a large
                   high resolution touch screen and inbuilt camera. Support various kinds of payment options, including
                   bank card payments, Near Field Communication (“NFC”) contactless and QR code payments.
                                    PCI PTS
       一般特點：       以安卓作業系統操作，並獲得        認証。外型小巧，方便手持，具有特大高清觸控屏及內置攝像
                                          NFC
                   頭。支援各種支付方式，包括銀行卡支付、       非觸式及二維碼支付等。

       UNATTENDED SOLUTIONS

       自助服務解決方案
       General features: Ideal for self-service sales points such as railway stations, petrol stations, parking lots and kiosks.
                   Products are certified with PCI PTS and have met required standards for anti-vandalism and
                   waterproofing. Support various kinds of payment options and connectivity options include 3G, 4G, WiFi
                   and Bluetooth.
                                                         PCI PTS

                                                各位股東：
       On behalf of the board of Directors (the “Board”) of PAX Global
                                                本人謹代表百富環球科技有限公司（「百富」或
       Technology Limited (“PAX” or “the Company”, together with its
                                                「本公司」，連同其附屬公司統稱「本集團」）董
       subsidiaries, the “Group”), I am pleased to present the annual report of
                                                事會（「董事會」），欣然提呈本集團截至二零
       the Group for the year ended 31 December 2023.
                                                二三年十二月三十一日止年度的年報。
       FINANCIAL RESULTS

       practices and establishes corporate governance procedures. With the

       The risk management and internal control systems of the Company

                                                而非消除未能達成業務目標的風險，而且只能

       up approach for identification, assessment and mitigation of risk at all

       斷，以及技術日新月異、客戶需求及競爭者之行為導致多
       種不明朗因素。

       獨立核數師報告


       Key Audit Matter                   How our audit addressed the Key Audit Matter

       關鍵審計事項                             我們的審計如何處理關鍵審計事項
                                          –  Tested on a sample basis, the NRV of selected inventory
                                             items, by comparing the selling price subsequent to the
                                             year end, against the carrying values of these individual
                                             finished goods. Where there are no subsequent sales
                                             of the respective finished goods after the year end, we
                                             discussed with management as to the realisable value
                                             of the products, corroborating explanations with the
                                             sales orders, historical margins, and current market
                                             conditions by using our industry knowledge and
                                             external market analysis, as appropriate.
                                          –
                                             以抽樣方式測試選定存貨項目之可變現淨值，在測試
                                             中將個別製成品於年末後的售價與其賬面值作一比
                                             較。對於年末後並無出售的相關製成品，我們已與管
                                             理層討論該產品的可變現值，並透過我們對行業的知
                                             識和外部市場分析（如適用），佐證有關銷售訂單、過
                                             往毛利率及現行市況的解釋。
                                          Based on the procedures described, we found the
                                          estimations of management in relation to the provision for
                                          inventories were supportable by available evidence.
                                          根據所述程序，我們發現管理層有關存貨撥備之估計有可
                                          得的證據支持。

          PAX Global Technology Limited (the “Company”) is an investment
                                                   百富環球科技有限公司（「本公司」）為一

                                                   間投資控股公司，連同其附屬公司（統稱

                                                   「本集團」）主要從事開發及銷售電子支
          development and sales of electronic funds transfer point-of-sale
                                                   付銷售點（「電子支付終端」）產品、提供維
          (“E-payment Terminals”) products, provision of maintenance and
                                                   護及安裝及支付解決方案服務（統稱「電
          installation and payment solution services (collectively, referred to
                                                   子支付終端解決方案業務」）。
          as the “E-payment Terminals solutions business”).
          The Company is a limited liability company incorporated in
                                                   本公司為一間在百慕達註冊成立的
          Bermuda. The address of its registered office is Clarendon House,
                                                   有限責任公司，其註冊辦事處地址為
          2 Church Street, Hamilton HM 11, Bermuda. Clarendon House, 2 Church Street,
                                                   Hamilton HM 11, Bermuda
                                                                   。

       3  FINANCIAL RISK MANAGEMENT             3
                                                   財務風險管理
          3.1 Financial risk factors               3.1
                                                      財務風險因素
             The Group’s activities expose it to a variety of financial risks:
                                                      本集團的活動使本集團承擔多種財
             market risk (including foreign exchange risk, price risk, cash
                                                      務風險：市場風險（包括外匯風險、
             flow interest rate risk and fair value interest rate risk), credit
                                                      價格風險、現金流利率風險及公平
             risk and liquidity risk. The Group’s overall risk management
                                                      值利率風險）、信貸風險及流動資金
             programme focuses on the unpredictability of financial
                                                      風險。本集團的整體風險管理計劃
             markets and seeks to minimise potential adverse effects on
                                                      針對金融市場的不可預測性，力求

          3.2 Capital management                   3.2
                                                      資本管理
             The Group regards its shareholders’ equity as capital. The
                                                      本集團將其股東權益視為資本。本
             Group’s objectives when managing capital are to safeguard
                                                      集團管理資本的目的為保障本集團
             the Group’s ability to continue as a going concern in order
                                                      能繼續以持續經營方式為股東提供
             to provide returns for shareholders and benefits for other
                                                      回報以及為其他利益相關者帶來利
             stakeholders and to maintain an optimal capital structure to
                                                      益，並且維持最佳資本結構以減少
             reduce the cost of capital.
                                                      資本成本。
             In order to maintain or adjust the capital structure, the
                                                      為維持或調整資本結構，本集團可
             Group may adjust the amount of dividends paid to
                                                      調整向股東支付股息的金額、將資
             shareholders, return capital to shareholders, issue new
                                                      本退還予股東、發行新股份、回購
             shares, repurchase the Company’s shares or sell assets to
                                                      本公司股份或出售資產以減少債
             reduce debt.
                                                      務。
             The Group monitors capital on the basis of gearing ratio.
                                                      本集團基於資本負債比率監控資
             This ratio is calculated as total debt divided by total capital.
                                                      本。該比率按債務總額除以資本總
             Total debt includes borrowings of the Group. Total capital is
                                                      額計算。債務總額包括本集團的借
             calculated as equity as shown in the consolidated balance
                                                      貸。資本總額為列於綜合資產負債
             sheet plus total debt.
                                                      表的權益加上債務總額計算。
             The Group did not have any borrowings as at 31 December
                                                      本集團於二零二三年十二月三十一
             2023 and the gearing ratio is not applicable (2022: same).
                                                      日並無借貸，資本負債比率並不適用
                                                      （二零二二年：同上）。

             The amount written off in the consolidated income

           (i) Revenue from sales of E-payment Terminals (i)

              products
              Revenue from sales of E-payment Terminals products are
                                                      銷售電子支付終端產品所得收入
              recognised when control of the products has transferred,
                                                      會於產品的控制權轉移時被確認，
              being when the products are delivered to the customers,
                                                      即當產品交付予客戶，且客戶已接
              the customer has accepted the products and there is no
                                                      納產品及無影響客戶接納產品的
              unfulfilled obligation that could affect the customer’s
                                                      未履行責任。
              acceptance of the products.
              A receivable is recognised when the goods are delivered

              unconditional because only the passage of time is required
                                                      逝除外）收到代價時，便可確認應
              before the payment is due.
                                                      收款項。
           (ii) Revenue from provision of services (ii)
                                                      提供服務所得收入
              Revenue from provision of services are recognised in the
                                                      提供服務所得收入會於提供服務

              period as a proportion of the total services to be provided
                                                      隨時間予以確認，因為客戶會在同
              because the customer receives and consumes the benefits
                                                      時間獲得及使用該利益。
              simultaneously.
           (iii) Contract liabilities              (iii)

              A contract liability is recognised when a customer

                                                      支付代價且金額已到期時確認。本

           Operating segments are reported in a manner consistent with

           for allocating resources and assessing the performance of
                                                   策者已被認定為作出策略決策的執行董
           the operating segments, has been identified as the Executive
                                                   事。
           Directors that make strategic decisions.
          The management reviews the Group’s internal reporting in order
                                                   管理層審閱本集團內部報告以評估表現
          to assess performance and allocate resources. The management
                                                   並分配資源。管理層根據由執行董事所
          has determined the operating segments based on the internal
                                                   審閱以作出策略決定的內部報告而釐定
          reports reviewed by the Executive Directors to make strategic
                                                   業務分類。本集團主要從事電子支付終
          decisions. The Group is principally engaged in the E-payment
                                                   端解決方案業務及管理層認為本集團經
          Terminals solutions business, and the management considers that
                                                   營單一業務分類。
          the Group operates in one single business segment.

                                                   司的位置評估本集團的表現及根據分類

          segmental operating profit/(loss).

       14 PROPERTY, PLANT AND EQUIPMENT         14
                                                   物業、廠房及設備
           Material accounting policy
                                                   重大會計政策
           Depreciation of property, plant and equipment is calculated using
                                                   物業、廠房及設備的折舊以直線法於其
           the straight-line method to allocate cost to their residual values
                                                   估計可用年期內分配其成本至剩餘價
           over their estimated useful lives, as follows:
                                                   值。所採用年率如下：
           Buildings            2% - 10%                       2% - 10%
                                                   樓宇
           Leasehold improvements 20% or over lease terms,     20%
                                                   租賃物業裝修         或按租賃年期
                                 whichever is shorter
                                                                （以較短者為準）
           Office furniture and equipment 18% - 25%            18% - 25%
                                                   辦公室傢俱及設備
           Plant and equipment  9% - 33%                       9% - 33%
                                                   廠房及設備
           Motor vehicles       18% - 25%                      18% - 25%
                                                   汽車
           No provision for depreciation is made on construction in progress
                                                   在相關資產完工並且可以用作擬定用途
           until such time as the relevant assets are completed and ready
                                                   前不會為在建工程計提折舊。
           for intended use.
           The assets’ residual values and useful lives are reviewed, and
                                                   資產的剩餘價值及可用年期會於各報告
           adjusted if appropriate, at the end of each reporting period.
                                                   期末審閱及調整（如適用）。

       15 RIGHT-OF-USE ASSETS AND LEASE LIABILITIES 15
                                                   使用權資產及租賃負債
           Material accounting policy
                                                   重大會計政策
           (i) Right-of-use assets                 (i)
                                                      使用權資產
              Right-of-use assets are generally depreciated over the
                                                      使用權資產一般於資產可用年期或
              shorter of the asset’s useful life and the lease term on
                                                      租賃期（以較短者為準）內按直線
              a straight-line basis. If the Group is reasonably certain
                                                      法予以折舊。倘本集團合理地確定
              to exercise a purchase option, the right-of-use asset is
                                                      會行使購買選擇權，則使用權資產
              depreciated over the underlying asset’s useful life.
                                                      於相關資產的可使用年期內予以折
                                                      舊。
           (ii) Lease liabilities                  (ii)
                                                      租賃負債
              Lease liabilities include the net present value of the
                                                      租賃負債包括固定租賃付款的淨現
              fixed lease payments. Lease payments to be made under
                                                      值。根據合理地確定會行使延續選
              reasonably certain extension options are also included in
                                                      擇權的租賃的租賃付款亦會計入其
              the measurement of the liability.
                                                      負債計量之內。
              The lease payments are discounted using the interest
                                                      租賃付款採用租賃所隱含的利率予
              rate implicit in the lease. If that rate cannot be readily
                                                      以貼現。倘無法輕易地釐定該利率
              determined, which is generally the case for leases in the
                                                      （為本集團租賃的一般情況），則使
              Group, the lessee’s incremental borrowing rate is used,
                                                      用承租人的增量借貸利率，即個別
              being the rate that the individual lessee would have to
                                                      承租人在類似經濟環境中按類似條
              pay to borrow the funds necessary to obtain an asset of
                                                      款、抵押及條件借入獲得與使用權
              similar value to the right-of-use asset in a similar economic
                                                      資產具有類似價值的資產所需的資
              environment with similar terms, security and conditions.
                                                      金而必須支付的利率。
              To determine the incremental borrowing rate, the Group,
                                                      為釐定增量借款利率，本集團在可
              where possible, uses recent third-party financing received
                                                      能情況下，使用個別承租人最近獲
              by the individual lessee as a starting point, adjusted to
                                                      得的第三方融資為出發點並作出調
              reflect changes in financing conditions since third party
                                                      整，以反映自獲得第三方融資以來
              financing was received and makes adjustments specific to
                                                      融資條件的變動，及進行特定於租
              the lease, e.g. term, country, currency and security.
                                                      賃的相關調整，例如期限、國家、貨
                                                      幣及抵押。

       16 INTANGIBLE ASSETS                     16
                                                   無形資產
           Material accounting policy
                                                   重大會計政策
           (i) Goodwill                            (i)
                                                      商譽
              Goodwill is not amortised but it is tested for impairment
                                                      商譽不會被攤銷，但會每年為其進
              annually, or more frequently if events or changes in
                                                      行減值測試，倘有事件或情況變化
              circumstances indicate that it might be impaired, and is
                                                      顯示商譽可能出現減值情況，則會
              carried at cost less accumulated impairment losses.
                                                      更頻密地進行測試。以及，商譽會
                                                      按成本減累計減值虧損列賬。
              Gains and losses on the disposal of an entity include the
                                                      出售實體的收益及虧損包括與被
              carrying amount of goodwill relating to the entity sold.
                                                      出售實體相關的商譽的賬面值。
              Goodwill is allocated to cash-generating units (“CGUs”)
                                                      商譽會被分配至現金產生單位
              for the purpose of impairment testing. The allocation is
                                                      （「現金產生單位」）以作減值測
              made to those cash-generating units or groups of cash-
                                                      試。該等預期因業務合併而受惠的
              generating units that are expected to benefit from the
                                                      現金產生單位或現金產生單位組
              business combination in which the goodwill arose. The
                                                      別將獲分配從而所產生的商譽。該
              units or groups of units are identified at the lowest level
                                                      等單位或單位組別被認定為就內
              at which goodwill is monitored for internal management
                                                      部管理目的而對商譽進行監督的
              purposes.

           Material accounting policy
                                                   重大會計政策
           Trade and bills receivables including retention money receivables

           expectation of recovery. Subsequent recoveries of amounts

           Material accounting policy
                                                   重大會計政策
           Trade payables are obligations to pay for goods or services that
                                                   應付賬款為於正常業務過程中從供應商
           have been acquired in the ordinary course of business from
                                                   取得商品或服務中須承擔的支付義務。
           suppliers.
           Trade and other payables are presented as current liabilities
                                                   如果付款期限少於一年（或如屬較長時
           if payment is due within one year or less (or in the normal
                                                   間，則於一般業務營運週期），應付賬款
           operating cycle of the business if longer). If not, they are
                                                   及其他應付賬款則被呈列為流動負債。
           presented as non-current liabilities.
                                                   否則，會被呈列為非流動負債。
           Trade and other payables are recognised initially at fair values
                                                   應付賬款及其他應付賬款會初始按公平
           and subsequently measured at amortised cost using the effective
                                                   值確認，其後使用實際利息法按攤銷成
           interest method.
                                                   本計量。

       28 DEFERRED INCOME TAX                   28
                                                   遞延所得稅
           Material accounting policy
                                                   重大會計政策
           Deferred income tax is provided in full, using the liability method,
                                                   遞延所得稅乃就資產與負債的稅基及其
           on temporary differences arising between the tax bases of assets
                                                   於綜合財務報表中的賬面值兩者間產生
           and liabilities and their carrying amounts in the consolidated
                                                   的暫時性差額，並以負債法悉數進行撥
           financial statements. However, deferred tax liabilities are not
                                                   備。然而，倘遞延稅項負債產生自商譽
           recognised if they arise from the initial recognition of goodwill.
                                                   的初始確認，則不會被確認。倘遞延所
           Deferred income tax is also not accounted for if it arises from
                                                   得稅乃產生自於交易（業務合併除外）中
           initial recognition of an asset or liability in a transaction other
                                                   對資產或負債的初始確認，而於交易當
           than a business combination that at the time of the transaction
                                                   時並無影響會計或應課稅溢利或虧損且
           affects neither accounting nor taxable profit or loss and does not
                                                   不產生相等金額的應課稅及可扣減的暫
           give rise to equal taxable and deductible temporary differences.
                                                   時性差額，亦不會被確認。遞延所得稅
           Deferred income tax is determined using tax rates (and laws)
                                                   乃以於報告期末已制定或實質上已制
           that have been enacted or substantially enacted at the end of
                                                   定，並預期於變現相關遞延所得稅資產
           the reporting period and are expected to apply when the related
                                                   或償還相關遞延所得稅負債時適用的稅
           deferred income tax asset is realised or the deferred income tax
                                                   率（及法例）釐定。
           liability is settled.
           Deferred tax assets are recognised only if it is probable that
                                                   遞延稅項資產只會於未來可能有應課稅
           future taxable amounts will be available to utilise those
                                                   金額可使用該等暫時性差額及虧損時方
           temporary differences and losses.
                                                   予以確認。
           Deferred tax liabilities and assets are not recognised for
                                                   當海外業務投資的賬面值及稅基產生暫
           temporary differences between the carrying amount and tax
                                                   時性差額，而本集團有能力控制暫時性
           bases of investments in foreign operations where the Group
                                                   差額撥回的時間點，且有可能不會在可
           is able to control the timing of the reversal of the temporary
                                                   見將來撥回時，遞延稅項負債及資產則
           differences and it is probable that the differences will not reverse
                                                   不會被確認。
           in the foreseeable future.

             (i) Subsidiaries                         (i)

          35.2 Business combinations               35.2
                                                      業務合併
             The acquisition method of accounting is used to account

             for all business combinations, regardless of whether equity
                                                      賬，無論所收購者為權益工具或其

                                                      他資產。收購一間附屬公司所轉讓

                business

             •  fair value of any asset or liability resulting from a •
                                                         或然代價安排所產生的任何資
                contingent consideration arrangement, and
                                                         產或負債的公平值；及
             •  fair value of any pre-existing equity interest in the •
                                                         於該附屬公司任何先前已存在
                subsidiary.
                                                         的權益的公平值
             Identifiable assets acquired and liabilities and contingent
                                                      除有限例外情況外，於業務合併所

          35.6 Impairment of non-financial assets  35.6
                                                      非金融資產的減值
             Goodwill is not subject to amortisation and is tested annually
                                                      商譽不會被攤銷並需要每年為其進
             for impairment, or more frequently if events or changes in
                                                      行減值測試，或倘有事件或情況變
             circumstances indicate that they might be impaired. Other
                                                      動表明其可能出現減值，則會更頻
             assets are tested for impairment whenever events or changes
                                                      繁地進行減值測試。其他資產須於
             in circumstances indicate that the carrying amount may not
                                                      指出其未必可收回賬面值的事件或
             be recoverable. An impairment loss is recognised for the
                                                      變動發生時測試減值。減值虧損為
             amount by which the asset’s carrying amount exceeds its
                                                      資產賬面值高於其可收回價值的金
             recoverable amount. The recoverable amount is the higher
                                                      額。可收回金額為資產的公平值減
             of an asset’s fair value less costs of disposal and value in
                                                      處置成本後的價值，與其使用價值
             use. For the purposes of assessing impairment, assets are
                                                      兩者中的較高者。為了評估資產減
             grouped at the lowest levels for which there are separately
                                                      值，本集團按可獨立地確認其現金
             identifiable cash inflows which are largely independent of
                                                      流入且其現金流入很大程度上獨立
             the cash inflows from other assets or groups of assets (cash-
                                                      於其他資產或資產組合的最低層次
             generating units). Non-financial assets other than goodwill
                                                      單位（現金產生單位）將資產分類。
             that suffered an impairment are reviewed for possible
                                                      除商譽外，已蒙受減值的非金融資
             reversal of the impairment at the end of each reporting
                                                      產在各報告期末均會就減值是否可
             period.
                                                      以撥回進行檢討。

          35.15 Provisions                         35.15
             Provisions are recognised when the Group has a present 撥備
             legal or constructive obligation as a result of past events, 當本集團因過往事件承擔現有法
             it is probable that an outflow of resources will be required 律或推定性責任，而履行責任有可
             to settle the obligation and the amount has been reliably 能導致資源的流出，且金額能夠可
             estimated. Provisions are not recognised for future operating 靠地估算的情況下，撥備便會被確
             losses.                                  認。未來經營虧損不會被確認為撥
                                                      備。
             Where there are a number of similar obligations, the
             likelihood that an outflow will be required in settlement 倘承擔若干類似責任，於釐定履行
             is determined by considering the class of obligations as a 責任導致資源流出的可能性時，將
             whole. A provision is recognised even if the likelihood of an 以整類責任類別作為整體予以考
             outflow with respect to any one item included in the same 慮。即使同類責任當中任何一項導
             class of obligations may be small.       致資源流出的可能性甚低，撥備亦
                                                      會被確認。
             Provisions are measured at the present value of
             management’s best estimate of the expenditures required 撥備以管理層於報告期末為履行現
             to settle the present obligation at the end of the reporting 有責任所需支出的最佳估算現值計
             period. The discount rate used to determine the present 量。計算此等現值使用的貼現率為
             value is a pre-tax rate that reflects current market 能夠反映當前市場的貨幣時間價值
             assessments of the time value of money and the risks 及該負債特有風險的稅前貼現率。
             specific to the liability. The increase in the provision due to 時間流逝導致撥備金額的增幅，會
             the passage of time is recognised as interest expense. 被確認為利息開支。
          35.16 Interest income                    35.16

          35.17 Leases (as lessee)                 35.17

             statement over the lease period so as to produce a constant

             liability for each period.
